        $(function () {
            $('a.btn[title]').tooltipHelp();

            if ($(window).width() > 930) {
                $('#skyscraper').show();

                $('body').addClass('skyscrapered');

                $(window).scroll(function() {
                    var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

                    var leaderBordTopPosition = $('#leaderboard-top').offset().top;

                    if (leaderBordTopPosition - scrollTop >= 10) {
                        $('#skyscraper').offset({
                            top: leaderBordTopPosition,
                            left: $('#skyscraper').offset().left
                        });
                    } else {
                        $('#skyscraper').offset({
                            top: scrollTop + 10,
                            left: $('#skyscraper').offset().left
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
        });

    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    /* global Zenbox */

    $(function () {
        if (GP.isBadBrowser()) {
            $('#oldBrowser').prepend($('<div class="old-browser">OldBrowserText. <a href="https://www.mozilla.org/de/firefox/new/">OldBrowserAction</a></div>'));
        }

        var isZenBoxInit = false, isLoading = false;

        $('#zendesk').click(function () {
            if (!isLoading) {
                if (isZenBoxInit) {
                    Zenbox.show();
                } else {
                    isLoading = true;

                    $('head').append('<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" href="https://assets.zendesk.com/external/zenbox/v2.6/zenbox.css" />');

                    $.getScript('https://assets.zendesk.com/external/zenbox/v2.6/zenbox.js', function () {
                        window.Zenbox.init({
                            url: "https://busliniensuche.zendesk.com",
                                dropboxID: "20303331",
                            hide_tab: true
                        });

                        isZenBoxInit = true;
                        isLoading = false;

                        Zenbox.show();
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function () {
            var cookieWarning = $('#cookie-warning');

            if (!$.cookie('CookieInfo')) {
                cookieWarning.show();

                cookieWarning.find('a.dismiss').click(function () {
                    cookieWarning.remove();

                    $.cookie('CookieInfo', 1, { expires: 365, path: "/" });
                });
            }
        });
    </script>
